Either way—whether the issue stems from the inner condition on `custom` or the outer condition on `defaults`—the solution is the same: `migrateOverrides` must execute regardless of whether these nested fields exist, which means it needs to sit outside both conditionals entirely. is a subtle bug I'm missing.\n\nLooking at processPanelsV38 again...
